country_event = { #Netherlands in 1936
	id = holst.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holst.1" }
	title = holst.1.t
	desc = holst.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_rhine_ships

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = hol_democrat
	}

	option = {
		name = holst.1.a
	}

	option = {
		name = holst.1.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		country_event = holst.10001
	}
}

	}

country_event = { #We zijn verloren :(
	id = hol.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hol.2" }
	#	title = hol.2.t
	#	desc = hol.2.d

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HOL
		is_subject = yes
		NOT = {
			OVERLORD = { has_country_flag = hol_vuile_bezetter }
		}
	}

	option = {
		clr_country_flag = hol_vnh_dictatorship
		clr_country_flag = hol_radicalright
		clr_country_flag = hol_cna_government

		clr_country_flag = hol_coalition_cna_vnh
		#clr_country_flag = hol_coalition_lsp_vnh
		clr_country_flag = hol_coalition_sdap_rsap
		clr_country_flag = hol_coalition_sdap_vdb
		clr_country_flag = hol_coalition_vnh_cna
		#clr_country_flag = hol_conlib_government
		#clr_country_flag = hol_conlibsoc_gov
		clr_country_flag = hol_democrat
		clr_country_flag = hol_dutch_republic
		#clr_country_flag = hol_farleft_majority
		#clr_country_flag = hol_farright_majority
		clr_country_flag = hol_junta_consolidated
		#clr_country_flag = hol_left_confessional
		#clr_country_flag = hol_liberal
		#clr_country_flag = hol_liberals
		clr_country_flag = hol_military_junta
		clr_country_flag = hol_nas_majority
		clr_country_flag = hol_patriotten_majority
		#clr_country_flag = hol_purple_government
		clr_country_flag = hol_putsch
		#clr_country_flag = hol_pvda_rules_alone
		#clr_country_flag = hol_pvdv_chu_rksp
		clr_country_flag = hol_radicalleft
		clr_country_flag = hol_radicalright
		clr_country_flag = hol_modleft
		clr_country_flag = hol_modright
		#clr_country_flag = hol_rainbow_cabinet
		clr_country_flag = hol_roman_red_government
		clr_country_flag = hol_rsap_majority
		#clr_country_flag = hol_rsap
		#clr_country_flag = hol_rutte_i
		#clr_country_flag = hol_sdap
		#clr_country_flag = hol_sdapmajority
		#clr_country_flag = hol_soc_liberals
		#clr_country_flag = hol_syndie
		clr_country_flag = hol_gele_kerken
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		load_focus_tree = HOL_focus
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = hol_vuile_bezetter
			}
			clr_country_flag = hol_vuile_bezetter
		}
		HOL = {
			set_country_flag = hol_vuile_bezetter_base
			OVERLORD = {
				set_country_flag = hol_vuile_bezetter
			}
		}
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Making sure you're not stuck with some council as a puppet
	id = hol.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hol.5" }

	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HOL
		is_subject = yes
	}

	option = { #mOETHIERZIJN
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Henk Sneevliet"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/HOL/Portrait_HOL_Sneevliet.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = moderate_socialist_subtype
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = HOL_Henk_Sneevliet_hog_rso
			add_ideas = HOL_Willem_van_Ravesteyn_for_rso
			add_ideas = HOL_Hermanus_Martinus_Peters_eco_rso
			add_ideas = HOL_Fokke_Bosman_sec_rso
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Harm Kolthek"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/HOL/Portrait_HOL_Kolthek.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = HOL_Harm_Kolthek_hog_syn
			add_ideas = HOL_Nicolaas_Beuzemaker_for_syn
			add_ideas = HOL_Jan_Postma_eco_syn
			add_ideas = HOL_Evert_Kupers_sec_syn
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = totalist
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Paul de Groot"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/HOL/Portrait_HOL_De_Groot.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authcom_subtype
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = HOL_David_Wijnkoop_hog_tot
			add_ideas = HOL_Paul_de_Groot_for_tot
			add_ideas = HOL_Louis_de_Visser_eco_tot
			add_ideas = HOL_Bernhard_Coltof_sec_tot
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Making sure you're not stuck with some council as a puppet
	id = hol.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hol.6" }

	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HOL
		has_socialist_government = yes
		is_in_faction_with = GER
		GER = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #mOETHIERZIJN
		name = hol.6.a
		GER = {
			remove_from_faction = HOL
		}
		set_country_flag = hol_has_been_syndie
	}
}

		remove_ideas = HOL_idea_agreement_with_right_0
		remove_ideas = HOL_idea_agreement_with_right_1
		remove_ideas = HOL_idea_agreement_with_right_2
		remove_ideas = HOL_idea_high_debts
		remove_ideas = HOL_idea_high_inflation
	}
}

country_event = { #event to set a flag which faction the government is in.
	id = hol.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event hol.8" }

	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HOL
		has_socialist_government = no
		is_in_faction = yes
		is_subject = no
	}

	option = {
		name = hol.7.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ENT
			}
			set_country_flag = holex_already_entente
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			set_country_flag = holex_already_reichspakt
		}
	}
}

		has_country_flag = hol_radicalleft
	}

	option = {
		name = holel.5.a #The financing of the crowning ceremony didn't pass
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}

		add_ideas = HOL_Charles_Guillaume_Cramer_sec_sde

			}

			limit = {

				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = BEL
				BEL = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			BEL = { dismantle_faction = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				var:faction_leader = { has_socialist_government = no }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Torching of the binnenhof
	id = holpostel.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holpostel.1" }
	title = holpostel.1.t
	desc = holpostel.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_binnenhof_fire

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = hol_modright
			has_country_flag = hol_radicalright
			has_country_flag = hol_junta_consolidated
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = hol_dont_burn_binnenhof
		}
	}

	option = { #Keep calm and carry on
		name = holpostel.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = HOL_election_1937
					option = HOL_ELECTION_1937_STATE_OF_EMERGENCY
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.15
		#add_political_power = -150
		set_country_flag = hol_binnenhof_burning
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = holpostel.2
					days = 2
				}
				} #Antisyndicalist riots
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = holpostel.86
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #declare state of emergency
		name = holpostel.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HOL_election_1937
						option = HOL_ELECTION_1937_SOCCON_MARLIB_LEFT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HOL_election_1937
						option = HOL_ELECTION_1937_SOCCON_MARLIB_RIGHT
					}

						rule = HOL_election_1937
						option = HOL_ELECTION_1937_SOCCON_ALONE

						rule = HOL_election_1937
						option = HOL_ELECTION_1937_SOCCON_VHN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HOL_election_1937

						rule = HOL_election_1937
						option = HOL_ELECTION_1937_SDAP_WIN_RSAP_OVERTHROW_SYSTEM_GERMAN_INTERVENTION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = HOL_election_1937

			}

		}

			}

					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

		if = {

		}

			}

			}
		}

				}
			}
		}
		INS = {

				has_idea = HOL_idea_high_inflation
			}
			remove_ideas = HOL_idea_high_inflation
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HOL_idea_high_debts
			}
			remove_ideas = HOL_idea_high_debts
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HOL_idea_workplace_regulations_cut
			}
			remove_ideas = HOL_idea_workplace_regulations_cut
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_subject = FLN }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FLN
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = BEL
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = BEL
				BEL = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			}
			BEL = { dismantle_faction = yes }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				var:faction_leader = { has_socialist_government = no }
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		country_event = holex.1 #Fate of the colonies
	}

	#	option = { #The revolting north shall be subdued
	#		name = holpostel.3.b

	}

				}
			}
		}

				has_idea = HOL_Benjamin_Lopes_Cardazo_for_syn
				has_idea = HOL_Henriette_Roland_Holst_sec_syn
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = HOL_Anton_Pannekoek_hog_syn
				has_idea = HOL_Henriette_Roland_Holst_sec_syn
				has_idea = HOL_Abraham_Verduin_eco_syn
			}
			AND = {
				has_idea = HOL_Henriette_Roland_Holst_sec_syn
				has_idea = HOL_Benjamin_Lopes_Cardazo_for_syn
				has_idea = HOL_Abraham_Verduin_eco_syn

		}
	}

			elections_allowed = no

		}

			popularity = 0.1
		}

			ideology = totalist
			name = HOL_council_communist
			long_name = HOL_council_communist_long
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Anton Pannekoek"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/HOL/Portrait_HOL_Anton_Pannekoek.png"

			ideology = bordigism_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = hol_cc_majority
		#complete_national_focus = HOL_council_of_the_state
	}
}

#ASW destroyer
country_event = {
	id = holnavy.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holnavy.1" }
	title = holnavy.1.t
	desc = holnavy.1.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_lichte_kruiser

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = holnavy.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = holnavy.1.a.tt
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = holnavy.1.t
			bonus = 1
			uses = 2
			category = dd_tech
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holnavy.1.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = holnavy.1.b.tt
		unlock_decision_tooltip = HOL_build_isaac_sweers_class
		unlock_decision_tooltip = HOL_build_isaac_sweers_class_2

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = basic_ship_hull_light
				can_research = improved_ship_hull_light
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Isaac Sweers Class"
				type = ship_hull_light_2
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_battery_1
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_1
					fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_1
					fixed_ship_engine_slot = light_ship_engine_2
					fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_1
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_1
					rear_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_2
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_asw_destroyer_2
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = improved_ship_hull_light
				can_research = advanced_ship_hull_light
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Isaac Sweers Class"
				type = ship_hull_light_3
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_battery_2
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_1
					fixed_ship_engine_slot = light_ship_engine_2
					fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_2
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_2
					rear_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_3
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_asw_destroyer_3
		}

		if = { limit = { has_tech  = advanced_ship_hull_light }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Isaac Sweers Class"
				type = ship_hull_light_4
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_battery_3
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_3
					fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2
					fixed_ship_engine_slot = light_ship_engine_3
					fixed_ship_torpedo_slot = ship_torpedo_2
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_3
					rear_1_custom_slot = ship_depth_charge_4
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_asw_destroyer_4
		}
	}
}

			set_country_flag = HOL_eendracht_cruiser_3_good
		}

		if = { limit = { has_tech  = advanced_ship_hull_cruiser }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Eendracht Class"
				type = ship_hull_cruiser_4
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_3
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2
					fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_engine_slot = cruiser_ship_engine_3
					fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = dp_light_battery_1
					fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_cruiser_1
					front_1_custom_slot =  ship_light_medium_battery_3
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					mid_2_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_3
					rear_1_custom_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_3
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_eendracht_cruiser_4_good
		}
	}
}

## AA-light cruiser
country_event = {
	id = holnavy.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holnavy.7" }
	title = holnavy.7.t
	desc = holnavy.7.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_torpedoboot

	option = {
		name = holnavy.7.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = holnavy.7.a.tt
		unlock_decision_tooltip = HOL_build_aa_cruisers
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = basic_ship_hull_cruiser
				can_research = improved_ship_hull_cruiser
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Jakob van Heemskerck Class"
				type = ship_hull_cruiser_2
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2
					fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_engine_slot = cruiser_ship_engine_2
					fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_cruiser_1
					front_1_custom_slot =  ship_anti_air_2
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_1
					mid_2_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					rear_1_custom_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_aa_cruiser_2
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = improved_ship_hull_cruiser
				can_research = advanced_ship_hull_cruiser
			}
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Jakob van Heemskerck Class"
				type = ship_hull_cruiser_3
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2

					fixed_ship_engine_slot = cruiser_ship_engine_3
					fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_cruiser_1
					front_1_custom_slot =  ship_anti_air_2
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_1
					mid_2_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
					rear_1_custom_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_1
					rear_2_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_2
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_aa_cruiser_3
		}

		if = { limit = { has_tech  = advanced_ship_hull_cruiser }
			create_equipment_variant = {
				name = "Jakob van Heemskerck Class"
				type = ship_hull_cruiser_4
				parent_version = 0
				modules = {
					#fixed_ship_battery_slot = dp_ship_light_medium_battery
					fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_3
					fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2
					fixed_ship_radar_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_engine_slot = cruiser_ship_engine_3
					fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = empty
					fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_cruiser_1
					front_1_custom_slot =  ship_anti_air_2
					mid_1_custom_slot = ship_torpedo_2
					mid_2_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_3
					#rear_1_custom_slot = dp_ship_light_medium_battery
					rear_2_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_3
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = HOL_aa_cruiser_4
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holnavy.7.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = holnavy.7.b.tt
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = holnavy.7.t
			bonus = 0.75
			uses = 1
			category = cl_tech

country_event = {
	id = holnavy.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holnavy.15" }
	title = holnavy.15.t
	desc = holnavy.15.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_torpedoboot

	option = {
		name = holnavy.15.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = holnavy.15.a.tt
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = holnavy.15.t
			bonus = 0.75
			uses = 2
			category = dd_tech
			category = cat_torpedoes

		}
	}

	option = {
		name = holnavy.15.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = HOL_destroyer_escort_tt
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = holnavy.15.t
			bonus = 0.75
			uses = 1
			category = dd_tech
			category = cat_torpedoes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = HOL_base_design_cl
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = HOL_base_design_cl
				add_idea = HOL_base_design_dd_cl
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = HOL_base_design_dd
			}
		}

	}
}

	title = holnavy.8.t
	desc = holnavy.8.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_torpedoboot

	option = { ## Upgrade the existing ships
		name = holnavy.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = holnavy.8.a.tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Aemila Class (Upgraded)"
					type = ship_hull_heavy_1
					parent_version = 0
					modules = {
						fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_heavy_battery_2
						fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_3
						fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2
						fixed_ship_engine_slot = heavy_ship_engine_2
						fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = ship_secondaries_1
						fixed_ship_armor_slot = ship_armor_bb_2
						front_1_custom_slot = ship_anti_air_3
						mid_1_custom_slot = ship_secondaries_2
						rear_1_custom_slot = ship_heavy_battery_2
					}
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Willem van Oranje Class (Upgraded)"
					type = ship_hull_heavy_2
					parent_version = 0
					modules = {
						fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_heavy_battery_3
						fixed_ship_anti_air_slot = ship_anti_air_3
						fixed_ship_fire_control_system_slot = ship_fire_control_system_2
						fixed_ship_radar_slot = ship_radar_1
						fixed_ship_engine_slot = heavy_ship_engine_3
						fixed_ship_secondaries_slot = ship_secondaries_2

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				set_technology = { basic_battlecruiser = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

## Airplane focus events

#Koolhoven Fighters - Improved firepower lower reliability
country_event = {
	id = holfocus.400
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holfocus.400" }
	title = holfocus.400.t
	desc = holfocus.400.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = holfocus.400.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"}
			if = {
				limit = { can_research = basic_small_airframe }
				set_technology = { basic_small_airframe = 1 }
				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Koolhoven FK.55-1"
					type = small_plane_airframe_1
					modules = {

#CAS or Tactical
country_event = {
	id = holfocus.402
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holfocus.402" }
	title = holfocus.402.t
	desc = holfocus.402.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = holfocus.402.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"}
			if = {
				limit = { can_research = basic_small_airframe }
				set_technology = { basic_small_airframe = 1 }
				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Fokker C.X."
					type = small_plane_cas_airframe_1
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = bomb_locks
						fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_1 = empty
						engine_type_slot = engine_2_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = empty
						special_type_slot_2 = empty
			}
			}
		}
			else_if = {
				limit = { can_research = improved_small_airframe }
				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Fokker C.X-3"
					type = small_plane_cas_airframe_1
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = bomb_locks
						fixed_auxiliary_weapon_slot_1 = empty
						engine_type_slot = engine_2_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = armor_plate_small

					name = "Fokker C.XIII-3"

						plane_engine_upgrade = 1

						plane_engine_upgrade = 1
					}
				}

	option = { #Join CEST
		name = holflavor.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
	option = { #Stay with GMT
		name = holflavor.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

	id = holflavor.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holflavor.6" }
	title = holflavor.6.t
	desc = holflavor.6.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Tell the truth
		name = holflavor.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

	option = { #Accuse syndicalists of causing the fire
		name = holflavor.6.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_political_power = -25
	}

	option = { #Accuse reactionaries of causing the fire
		name = holflavor.6.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = totalist
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_political_power = -25
	}
}

country_event = { #First VNH Landdag since seizing power
	id = holflavor.11
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event holflavor.11" }
	title = holflavor.11.t
	desc = holflavor.11.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = HOL
		has_country_flag = hol_radicalright
		OR = {
			AND = {
				date > 1937.09.01
				date < 1937.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1938.09.01
				date < 1938.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1939.09.01
				date < 1939.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1940.09.01
				date < 1940.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1941.09.01
				date < 1941.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1942.09.01
				date < 1942.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1943.09.01
				date < 1943.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1944.09.01
				date < 1944.09.30
			}
			AND = {
				date > 1945.09.01
				date < 1945.09.30
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = national_populist
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
		}
	}

	option = { #Hou zee!
		name = holflavor.11.a
		set_country_flag = first_landdag
	}
}
